Procedure:

i. Identify those activities, operation and services that are having hazards and risk
assessed and identified and prioritized significant risks where operational control is
required.

ii. Documented operational control procedures shall be prepared to cover the activities,
operations and services.

iii. Operational Control Procedures shall be made available at the place of work in printed
or electronic form.

iv. Critical equipment, machinery and other sources from point of OH & S shall be
identified and their preventive maintenance schedule shall be laid down in order to
reduce / control or prevent incidents. Machines and equipment shall be operated,
monitored as per the Operational Control Procedures and laid down criteria and
records shall be maintained.

v. Controls related to contractors for adherence to all safety precautions and applicable
guidelines.

13.0 Safety Guidelines by Ministry of Steel;

The Contractor shall adopt the Safety guidelines issued by Ministry of Steel while

working at site, the guidelines are available in the following website;

https://steel.gov.in/safety/safety-guidelines-iron-steel-sector

Annexure-1C (contd.)
Note:
1. When an injury occurs to aContractor’s employee while inside the factory, the injured
person should be sent to Plant Medical Unit immediately, with this form in triplicate.
2. The Medical Officer on duty at Plant Medical Unit will retain one copy and send one copy
to Safety Engineering Department. The third copy shall be returned to the Contractor
concerned after duly filling up the forms.
In case, the Contractor takes the injured person to his private doctor, he shall do so by
giving a written undertaking to the doctor in Plant Medical Unit and to the Manager, Safety
Engineering Department.
If the private doctor declares the injured person unfit for duty more than 2 days, this
becomes a reportable accident under the Factories Act and the Contractor shall
immediately report this to the Manager, Safety Engineering Department for sending
reports to concerned Government agencies.
The Contractor shall also keep the manager (Safety) inform about :
a) The condition of the injured person ;
b) The period of disability and
c) Any loss of earning capacity certified by the doctor.
The Contractor shall produce the fitness certificate from the attending doctor after the
injured person is declared fit for duty.

NMDC
1. Scope of Work
1.1 This scope of work in this tender includes
To provide all the services (onsite support) required for successful and uninterrupted day to
day operations/transactions, maintenance, update and upgrade of the SAP ERP System at all
locations for the following modules of SAP S/4 HANA and entire SAP landscape implemented in
NMDC Limited including developments to be made as per the requirements of business notified
from time to time.
a) FINANCE & CONTROLLING (FICO)
b) MATERIALS MANAGEMENT (MM)
c) PRODUCTION PLANNING (PP)
d) PLANT MAINTENACE (PM)
e) HUMAN CAPITAL MANAGEMENT (HCM) / EMPLOYEE SELF SERVICE (ESS) /
MANAGEMENT SELF SERVICE (MSS)
f) PROJECT SYSTEM (PS)
g) SALES & DISTRIBUTION (SD)
h) QUALITY MANAGEMENT (QM)
i) ENVIRONMENT, HEALTH & SAFETY (EHS)
j) ADVANCED BUSINESS APPLICATION PROGRAMMING (ABAP)
k) BUSINESS APPLICATION SYSTEMS INTEGRATED SOLUTION (BASIS)
1) MANAGEMENT DASHBOARDS, FIORI APPS
1.2 Support shall be extended from Head Office, Hyderabad to all locations. The major locations
of NMDC are mentioned hereunder for information:
+ BIOM, Kirandul Complex, Dantewada. (Chhattisgarh)
+ BIOM, Bacheli Complex, Dantewada. (Chhattisgarh)
+ DIOM, Donimalai, Bellary (Karnataka)
+ Pellet Plant, Donimalai, Bellary (Karnataka)
+ DMP, Panna. (Madhya Pradesh)
+ SIU, Paloncha (Andhra Pradesh)
+ Slurry Pipe Line (SPL), Jagdalpur, (Chhattisgarh)
+ R&D Centre, Hyderabad (Telangana)
+ Regional Offices Delhi, Raipur, Visakhapatnam, Chennai, Bengaluru, Mumbai, Bhubaneshwar,
Kolkata.
However, wherever required, the support team has to travel to respective locations as per the
instructions of ERP GM(Mining)-ERP. The Conveyance, Lodging & Boarding charges will be borne by
NMDC as per the terms mentioned in this tender.

s CONTRACT - NMDC

NMDC
To take over and Knowledge Transfer of the SAP ERP System, software developments, source /
software codes, drawings, documents, manuals, reports, transactions & maintenance records etc.
from the Existing Contractor.

1.3 The major locations of NMDC are mentioned SPECIFIC REQUIREMENT:

i. The successful bidder is required to provide technical & functional support services which
include the identification and rectification of all defects/bugs.

ii, The successful bidder is required to assist in providing solution for recovery from transaction
errors, system errors, hardware failures and/or other application, modification,
enhancement issues etc.

iii. The successful bidder is required to assist in performing period end closing activities
(Monthly, Quarterly, and Annually) including Tax reporting, Regulatory Compliance etc.

iv. The support team should be based full time at NMDC Head Office, Hyderabad to facilitate
timely resolution of issues.

v. Enhancements, patches, version upgrades, service packs etc. (as applicable) are to be installed
time to time where ever required on release by OEM in consultation with the company
including third party solutions implemented and integrated with SAP. Each upgrade should be
accompanied by a detailed document containing the step by step procedure for effecting the
changes to the system by ensuing an established change management process.

vi. The successful bidder shall review and adopt the Governance, Risk & Compliance (GRC) in the
system to streamline and have better control across the transactions of the company.

vii. The successful bidder shall provide contact numbers, email addresses, escalation matrix of a
dedicated support team. NMDC shall be kept informed well in advance in case any changes are
being made in the contact details.

viii. The successful bidder shall submit detailed documentation (e.g. Technical documents,
Configuration documents, Functional document if any) for each resolved issue GM(Mining)-
ERP, NMDC Limited.

ix. The Dashboards developed and configured through Qlik Sense Software. The Scope of support
comprises maintenance of existing Dashboards including addition / deletion / modification of
specific views as per the business requirements.

x. For changes pertaining to completely new processes, or any new developments including
Dashboards etc., the total efforts (man days) required for the change requests will be mutually
agreed by both the successful bidder and NMDC. If the total efforts required are not more than
5-man days, then the successful bidder will implement the change free of cost. In case of
changes requiring efforts more than 5-man days, NMDC LIMITED will obtain a management
approval for the financial implication to carry out the changes. The financial implication will
be calculated by reducing the agreed effort by 5-man days and then multiplying the balance

man days with the rate (per man days) quoted in the commercial/price bid by the successful
bidder. It also includes integration with third party software planned in future, if any.

xi. The successful bidder has to develop a tracking system Module Wise to record the issues from
“raising of ticket” by the user / ERP Module Core Member till providing resolution.

xii. Computers/laptops for office work of staff of successful bidder shall be in the scope of
successful bidder. All other services required to administer, maintain, update and upgrade the
SAP ERP System as per standard of performance described in the Tender are included in the
scope of Services of successful bidder.

xiii. The successful bidder will maintain the SAP ERP System in such manner so as to minimize
operating cost and maximize the system availability.

xiv. The successful bidder has to prepare various documents including Administration Manual,
User Manuals, Standard Operating Procedure, Standard Maintenance Procedure, etc for SAP
ERP System and SAP Software.

xv. The successful bidder shall submit all the necessary documentation (i.e., Functional Specs,
Technical Specs, List of affected codes, Test Scripts, Unit Test Plans, System Test Plans etc) for
any changes they perform in the system. All these documents should be approved by NMDC
Limited.

xvi. The successful bidder also has to provide all temporary work, ancillary work, enabling work
etc including provision of tools & software required for performing Services.

xvii. The successful bidder shall provide adequate training as well as awareness programs to all
users in respective modules or as and when requested by NMDC without impacting the day to
day transactions.

xviii. The Basis Consultants of the successful bidder will perform all type of monitoring and
administrative activities like restarting SAP servers, maintenance of backup data,
maintenance of system configuration, administration for Browser-Based User Dialogs, User
Administration (ABAP/JAVA/PYTHON etc.), Creating and maintaining Remote Function Call
(RFC) Connections, Administration and Maintenance for External Communication, Schedule
Background Tasks, Printer and spool administration / maintenance, Administration and
maintenance of Transport Management System, System Monitoring and Trouble Shooting,
Setting Up an SAP System Landscape, SLD monitoring, Exporting/importing Transport
Requests, , System Workload Analysis, System trace monitoring, Performance Analysis, SAP
Memory Management , System Load Verification, Expensive SQL Statements Analysis, SAP
Table buffering, Database Overview and monitoring, DB Monitoring Tools, Recovery, DBA
activity through BR* Tools, RESTORING a BACKUP without any additional cost to NMDC
LIMITED.

xix. The successful bidder will perform SAP BASIS activities in Development, Quality and
production SAP S/4 HANA systems. They will also perform all the System Monitoring and
health check activities for smooth running of the servers.

xx. The successful bidder shall prepare weekly/monthly status reports and submit to NMDC
LIMITED.
xxi. The successful bidder shall take up any SAP product level issues with SAP through respective
module lead of NMDC and shall also follow up on the same for quick resolution.

xxii. If any support is required pertaining to SAP applications in DC & DR sites then same shall be
extended by the successful bidder to the DATA CENTER (DC) & DISASTER RECOVERY (DR) site
without any additional cost.

xxiii. The successful bidder will follow the holiday calendar of NMDC LIMITED. They have to work
late after working hours and attend issues on weekends/holidays as and when required
without any additional cost to NMDC LIMITED.

xxiv. Successful bidder shall keep each & every record, logs of the proceedings of each phases of the
project in writing to avoid any debatable issues of delaying the project on accounts of reasons
attributable to both the sides

xxv. Successful bidder shall submit monthly detailed report to GM(Mining)-ERP NMDC Limited on
Helpdesk ticket analysis with all status, Change Request status and status of all service
requests logged with OEM SAP and also make suitable presentation to the management on the
above issues as and when required. Additionally, successful bidder may share their comments
on quality of tickets, any major issues encountered & resolved, transactional difficulties and
adoption of best practices to help in reducing the tickets volume further.

xxvi. All the equipments, systems, and structures of the SAP ERP System will be maintained in the
form and condition as handed over to it by the Existing Contractor during the Takeover Phase
and it will provide services in relation to all these equipments, systems, and structures of the
SAP ERP System as per the said condition during the period of contract without any additional
cost to the NMDC and requesting any document from the NMDC evidencing performance
parameters of the SAP ERP System at the time of handover from the Existing Contractor.

xxvii. The scope of Services shall also include all such services which may not have been specifically
mentioned in this Tender, or the Technical Specifications, or the Functional Specifications but
which may be necessary for the successful fulfilment of Contractor's obligation mentioned in
this Tender as per Prudent Operating and Maintenance Practices and such services shall be
performed by the successful bidder without any additional cost to the NMDC.

Module wise minimum resource requirement for annual support services is mentioned

hereunder. However, if any additional resources are required the successful bidder has to

deploy the additional resources free of cost to address the issue without impacting the

business transactions:

PROJECT MANAGER (LEAD CONSULTANT)

FINANCE & CONTROL (FICO)

12. BUSINESS APPLICATION SYSTEMS INTEGRATED SOLUTION 2
(BASIS)
MANAGEMENT DASHBOARDS
= The above resource requirement is exclusively for support services, in respect of additional
developments (CR) mentioned in the Sl. No.2 of the Price Schedule, the successful bidder has
to provided separate resources at Head Office (or other places as required).
= NMDC management may take interview at the time of deployment. Any change in staff will be
done based on mutually agreement.
= If any of the deployed resource is unable to attend for work for any day, the successful bidder
has to provide suitable resource immediately with the approval of GM(Mining)-ERP. If any
resource is absent for more than 2 days and not been provided additional equivalent resource
as stated above, an amount equal to per man-day cost quoted at S]. No.2 of the price schedule
will be recovered / deducted from the monthly bill payable to the successful bidder. However,
if NMDC feels that such absenteeism is impacting the progress of work, NMDC reserves the
right to take action like termination of contract.
= The successful bidder will follow the holiday calendar of NMDC Limited. They should deploy
the resources during all the working days of NMDC Limited from Monday to Saturday (9:30
AM to 6:00 PM). The successful bidder team has to work late after working hours to address
the issues on weekends/holidays as and when required without any additional cost.

Administrators, Developers, Developers (Interface), Management
Reporting). Certification in the ERP function of the respective technical
lead is essential.
1.4 SCOPE OF WORK for SAP Support Service
The broad scope of the Functional and Technical consultant for SAP Support Services including
enhancement / customization of the SAP application in NMDC mentioned hereunder. It may note
that the scope mentioned hereunder is not exhaustive:

Role of SAP Functional Consultant

e Assist business users for the problems/issues encountered during day-to-day business
transactions for smooth functioning of the ERP System.

e Study and evaluate NMDC’s users’ requirements by interacting with the Core Team Members
& User Departments of NMDC and transform the essence into an abstract and algorithmic
business model or System Requirement Specifications.

e Realize the solution through standard features of SAP, if standard feature or alternative solution
is not available, solution may be provided through configuration and customizing the respective
business area and ensure to map the system to achieve the business requirements

e Provide the Documentation for the settings and Standard Operating Procedures (SOP) that allow
other consultants to do further changes or modifications if required.

e Providing proper training to the Users and Core Team Members where ever required.

e Functional consultants are also expected to prepare test scripts for testing the configured
scenarios in respect of new developments to be made.

e Preparation of the documents like As-is-study, Business Blue Print along with gap analysis and
get it approved through Core Team Members before starting to configuration of future business
processes in SAP.

e Performing minor Configuration changes to resolve existing business processes in line with the
problem on hand.

Role of SAP Technical Support: ABAP

e Bug Fixing (Program errors, Incorrect data display, etc.)

e Modifications to any custom objects to accommodate addition of new fields, selection
criterion, data display as long as this doesn’t result into a major code change

e Maintenance of Customized Transactions

e Performance tuning

e SAP Note applications

e Handling of Application Integration issues that fall in the purview of SAP

e Working closely with functional teams

e Support in analyzing & resolving the dump issues reported by the users

BASIS

e — Review and Analyse Daily, Weekly and Annual System Monitoring Checks.

e Assignment of Roles and Authorisations to end users as per approval regularly without delay
to ensure no business transactions was halted for want of Roles & Authorisations. (Like: CTS
move, User & Profile assignment and small correction in profile)

e Troubleshoot and rectify the problems on day-to-day basis

e Client copy / system refresh (whenever required at least once in a year)

e SAP note applications with reference to SAP Basis

e SNC configuration (whenever required at least once ina year).

e Handling of Application Integration issues that fall in the purview of SAP Basis

e Performance Tuning on Periodic Basis

e Support will be extended for Data Migrations for the approved change requests. The upload
data formats will be provided by the Consultants. NMDC will provide the cleansed and
validated data to the Support team.
